The answer is the walls:

A word of power, a word of might.
All the letters are here, within plain sight.

The word will make little sense, to those with a closed mind.
Open your eyes to words unknown, or those of quicker wit, will leave you behind.

Speak it and the way shall open, a doorway in the western wall.
Six little letters and the stones will fall.

Concentration is the key, follow the path out of this tower to see the way.
A keen mind will see the letters fall into place, a word shall converge.
A weak mind will see nothing but glare, the letters will spin and fray.
If you keep your head, return and speak the word, a doorway will emerge.
